You’ll receive 30 days of email support once you sign up, but after that you’re on your own. You’ll receive no phone, no email, or no chat support.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Not everybody has a creative background and can build emails or landing pages that look amazing and can convert, so they rely on the templates provided by their email marketing provider. With MailChimp, you only have access to their “basic” templates.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>And while MailChimp’s free plan has some advantages, MailChimp can quickly begin getting pricey as you begin growing your business and need more support and features.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">ConvertKit</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92007,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-ConvertKit-1024x256.png\" alt=\"ConvertKit Logo\" class=\"wp-image-92007\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ConvertKit is an email marketing service provider that’s built by a blogger for bloggers, although the platform is not limited to bloggers. The free plan starts at 100 subscribers for free, but that can jump to 1,000 through their referral program where you can earn an additional 100 subscribers for every referral who also signs up for a ConvertKit account.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">ConvertKit’s Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>On ConvertKit’s pricing comparison page they state their free tools as including:</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Landing page builder</li><li>Form builder</li><li>Segmentation</li><li>Subscriber tagging</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">ConvertKit Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The biggest pro that I can find with this platform is a tool that is not yet released. ConvertKit recently announced a brand new tool called ConvertKit Commerce. This feature will let you sell digital products right inside ConvertKit’s platform.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Outside of ConvertKit Commerce, there aren’t many pros to ConvertKit’s platform that you couldn’t find in other email service providers.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>They provide free migration services, so if you need to move from another email marketing platform, they will assist in moving you to ConvertKit. But you will need to have 5,000+ subscribers for it to be worth their time and effort.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">ConvertKit Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>ConvertKit is a very basic platform. There are no drag-and-drop email templates or builders. In fact, you only have two templates to choose from — a plain text version and a very plain-looking HTML version. And with the HTML version, you are limited with what you can customize.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The free plan also does not include email automation, which can be frustrating if you want to begin cultivating a relationship with your clients by sending welcome or thank you emails.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>While their landing page builder may be fully customizable, you have far fewer templates to choose from compared to other email marketing platforms such as AWeber.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>And they outsource their customer support so it can take hours to days for you to get a response.&#160; There is no email or phone support, instead you leave a message in their app and someone will email you a response.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Overall, ConvertKit lacks the bells and whistles that you can get with most other free email marketing services like MailChimp and AWeber.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">SendInBlue</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92013,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-SendInBlue-1024x256.png\" alt=\"Sendinblue logo\" class=\"wp-image-92013\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendInBlue was actually founded as a digital agency. They switched to become an email marketing provider when they realized an opportunity to help marketers automate email marketing on a budget.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendInBlue is a good tool for ecommerce marketers with customized triggers based on purchase behavior and the ability to import customer orders.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">SendInBlue Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>While SendInBlue has some very good email marketing features, many of those are only available with their paid plans. Their automation features are advanced and user-friendly. In fact, they are able to track your customers’ website behavior and trigger an email message at just the right time.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendInBlue’s email builder is also a very easy and convenient tool to use. You have the option to use one of their 140 email templates, or you can build your email campaign with their easy-to-use drag-and-drop editor.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">SendInBlue Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>While SendInBlue is a solid email marketing platform with good tools, they still lack a number of features you can get with other email providers. And they save their core features for their paid customers. You need to be on the Essential plan to start getting some of the real, juicy features, such as A/B testing, more detailed reporting, and better support.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendInBlue is also limited in the number of integrations with their platform.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Despite these limitations, the biggest con for the SendInBlue platform would have to be their daily email send limit. While you can have an unlimited number of subscribers, you can only send 300 emails a day, up to 9,000 for the month. Their email campaigns were easy to set up and use. They cater to small businesses, as roughly 90% of their subscribers have 50 employees or less.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">MailerLite Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The MailerLite free email plan includes access to features like automation, landing pages, and advanced segmentation. You don’t need a technical background to set up and send emails. And their email campaign reports are clear and easy to understand.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You also get full access to their marketing automation options which is a convenient option for those more sophisticated marketers.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>They also have a popup creator which you can have set up and ready to go with just a few clicks.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">MailerLite Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>While the reporting and email setup are really easy to use and navigate, their segments and grouping can be pretty confusing.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>And like so many other email marketing platforms we evaluated, you can only build up to 5 landing pages. And they have a very limited number of email and landing page templates. If you don’t have a creative background, you may find this very frustrating.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">MailJet</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92011,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-MailJet-1024x256.png\" alt=\"MailJet logo\" class=\"wp-image-92011\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If your main goal is to find a solid platform that is cheap once you graduate past the free plan, then MailJet may be for you. MailJet is one of the most basic email service providers that we researched, especially when it comes to their free email plan.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">MailJet Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>MailJet’s free email marketing features are very, very limited. Like SendInBlue, you won’t have to worry about upgrading your account as your subscribers increase, since you get unlimited contacts. However, also like SendInBlue, they limit you to a certain number of sends per day.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Other features in the free plan include:</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>API’s, SMTP Relay, Webhooks</li><li>An advanced email editor</li><li>Advanced statistics</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">MailJet Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The pros for the free email platform are few and far between. There’s obviously the unlimited contacts, which is a big plus. They also have a very easy to use drag-and-drop editor which is great for a new user. Outside of that, we didn’t find too many pros that would separate MailJet from the competition.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>One pro worth noting is a multi-user collaboration feature, which allows multiple users to work together in real-time on the same email. Think Google Docs. However, this is only available on the Premium or Enterprise paid programs.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">MailJet Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>MailJet is a very basic email service provider with no added benefits outside of email sending. Many of the other email marketing companies we reviewed have extra features such as a landing page builder or pop up builder. These extra features could be important as you look to grow your business and save money in the process.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>And, as mentioned above, although you can have unlimited contacts, MailJet does limit the number of emails you can send in a day to only 200 or a max of 6,000 per month. You may find it tough to grow your business sending to only 200 a day.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">Moosend</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92012,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-moosend-1024x256.png\" alt=\"Moosend logo\" class=\"wp-image-92012\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you’re looking for a platform with email automation options, but don’t need landing pages as an option for collecting subscribers, then it might be worth checking out Moosend.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">Moosend Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Moosend is relatively new when it comes to providing free email marketing services. And the available features are on par with some of the more well known platforms.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Unlimited emails</li><li>Sign up and subscription forms</li><li>Reporting and analytics</li><li>Drag-and-drop editor</li><li>Email automation</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">Moosend Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Moosend’s free email marketing platform offers a number of features not offered on other free platforms. Marketing automation features like onboarding and abandoned cart sequences and list segmentation, a/b testing options and spam testing are available.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Moosend’s Drag-and-Drop builder and templates also help email marketers get started with email design without worrying about coding.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">Moosend Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Moosend’s platform allows up to 1,000 unique subscribers on the free tier. However, when your subscriber count starts to climb, so does Moosend’s cost.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Other typically important features like the ability to send transactional emails and create landing pages are missing from Moosend’s free email platform. Phone support is also left out of the free plan, and is reserved for enterprise level users.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">SendPulse</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92014,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-sendpulse-1024x256.png\" alt=\"SendPulse logo\" class=\"wp-image-92014\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you’re looking for a marketing automation platform that lets you do more than just email, SendPulse has options for you. SendPulse offers SMS messaging, transactional email capabilities, chatbots and web push notifications.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">SendPulse Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendPulse has a good number of available tools, including:</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Email marketing automation</li><li>Web push notifications</li><li>SMS marketing</li><li>Viber marketing</li><li>Chatbot messaging</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">SendPulse Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>SendPulse lets you send up to 15,000 emails to 500 subscribers. However, the free plan limits the number of sender addresses you can have. Plus, while SendPulse offers some cool features like its Automation360 tool and the ability to resend to subscribers who haven’t opened your messages, SendPulse limits the storage volume for files up to 20Mb.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">SendPulse Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>In addition to the limited sender addresses and storage volume, SendPulse doesn’t allow you to bulk manage email addresses — i.e. you can’t export your mailing lists to Excel or other spreadsheets. And if you want to use SendPulse because of its SMS capabilities, you should know that you can only send 10 free SMS text messages through its free plan.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">EmailOctopus</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92008,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-EmailOctopus-1024x256.png\" alt=\"EmailOctopus logo\" class=\"wp-image-92008\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>EmailOctopus has a solid sender reputation with emails being sent through Amazon SES. Once you move past the free version, EmailOctopus is fairly affordable, but you get what you pay for in terms of features. If all you need are basic email features, then this email marketing service provider worth considering.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">EmailOctopus Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>They don't have a large number of features, but those they do have are solid.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Email marketing automation</li><li>Segmentation</li><li>Sign up forms</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">EmailOctopus Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Yes, EmailOctopus has one of the more generous free plans in terms of subscriber count. Free users can send 10,000 emails each month to up to 2,500 contacts, which is great if you want to send a weekly newsletter. Plus, with an easy-to-use WISIWYG email builder, creating good looking email newsletters isn’t difficult.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">EmailOctopus Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>EmailOctopus’ simplicity — which some could view positively — is also one of its main downsides. Their feature set is extremely limited and their usability is not that strong.&#160; The tool also stores your statistics for only 30 days at a time.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>So, if you want to take a more strategic approach to email marketing beyond weekly newsletters and analyze your email marketing results, it may be best to look elsewhere.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">BenchMark</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92005,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ESP-benchmark-1024x256.png\" alt=\"Benchmark logo\" class=\"wp-image-92005\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>BenchMark provides a simple email marketing service, but that's just how they want it. They designed their email builder to be simple and straightforward. Their email editor is super easy to use, one definitely doesn’t need a technical background to use this feature.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>They pride themselves on being international as they have a presence in fifteen countries around the world. Plus, from a useability standpoint, BenchMark gets it right.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">BenchMark Free Email Marketing Tools</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you are just starting out with email sending and have a very small email list, then the available features may work for you. However, compared to the competition, BenchMark’s available features on their free plan are very lite.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Basic Email Marketing</li><li>Lite Marketing Automation</li><li>Signup Forms</li><li>Basic Drip Campaigns</li><li>Heatmap reporting</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">BenchMark Email Platform Pros</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>BenchMark’s biggest pro is their, as they put it, insanely simple drag &#38; drop editor. And you’ll get no argument from me. This editor is as simple as it gets.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Automation Pro is a tool developed by Benchmark Email to create automations for your email subscribers. Automations are a set of elements or modules that automatically perform specific tasks based on your subscribers’ interactions with your emails and website. Within Automation Pro, automations can add or remove subscribers from lists or automatically send an email based on website activity, which are tasks that regular automations can’t do.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Their heatmap reporting is a nice touch for the more sophisticated marketer. And they have a basic, but solid marketing automation tool where you can set up simple behavior-based email campaigns.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">BenchMark Email Platform Cons</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>As nice of a platform the BenchMark has to offer, they have their cons. For starters, you can only send 250 emails per month. I don’t know about you, but that’s not enough for me to send one email to my list.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The free plan is also missing a lot of key features needed to grow your business such as their landing page builder, more advanced email automation, and priority support.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">So, how do you decide what’s right for you?</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>We know, that’s a lot to take in. But putting in the time upfront to figure out what email marketing service is best for you will pay off in the long run. Just want a quick comparison of the most important features? Check out the table we put together at the top of this article.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Ultimately, make sure you choose a provider who has — and will — stand the test of time. While migrating to AWeber from another platform is painless, we can’t promise the same for the other guys. So do your due diligence upfront to make sure you’re choosing a platform that’s powerfully-simple and gives you the features you need now and in the future.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- 08:20:11","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 08:20:11","title":"How to Promote Your Landing Page and Grow Your Email List","link":"https://blog.aweber.com/?p=91379","description":"<p><img width=\"1200\" height=\"675\" src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ht-promote-landing-page-grow-list_featured-and-social-1200x675-1.jpg\" class=\"attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image\" alt=\"How to Promote Your Landing Page\" srcset=\"http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ht-promote-landing-page-grow-list_featured-and-social-1200x675-1.jpg 1200w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ht-promote-landing-page-grow-list_featured-and-social-1200x675-1-300x169.jpg 300w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ht-promote-landing-page-grow-list_featured-and-social-1200x675-1-1024x576.jpg 1024w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/ht-promote-landing-page-grow-list_featured-and-social-1200x675-1-768x432.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p><!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You know that an awesome landing page is the first step to growing your list, selling more, and building relationships with your audience.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>So, you built one. You took time to <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/copywriting/write-sales-landing-pages.htm\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">write convincing landing page copy</a>. You’re ready to send your new subscribers value-packed emails. But there’s one problem.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>How do you actually get<em> </em>people <em>to</em> your landing page to sign up?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>That’s why we asked three experts to share how they drive traffic to their landing pages, and they shared some of the best strategies to help you begin promoting your own landing page. Read on to learn what they had to say.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Social media is a great way to promote your landing page — as long as you’ve built credibility first.</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Sam Flynn, Social Media Trainer &#38; Speaker, Managing Director, Planet Social Media</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Social media is a perfect driver of traffic to your landing page. </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The first step is to make sure you are clear on who your social media audience is. Once you have a good idea, think about what would drive them to want to go to your landing page. Is there a lead magnet that is highly relevant ? And, how can you get this across to them? </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>In terms of your call-to-action (CTA), you will need more than a simple “click here to get x.” Be more descriptive of the benefits behind this particular lead magnet. Give them value in the post itself, such as one of the points covered on your lead magnet, then direct them to your landing page for more.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You could also use video as part of your strategy, sharing a short video elaborating on one point covered in your lead magnet, then directing them to your lead magnet to get the remaining points. If you are speaking to a camera, be sure to include subtitles, for accessibility for all and to cater for those who will listen without audio.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Finally, make sure you build up your credibility with your audience by sharing a range of posts, especially those that demonstrate your expertise. They’ll be far more likely to click through to your landing page if they think they are going to get results from doing so!</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>When done right, Search Engine Optimization (SEO) is the best way to drive traffic to your landing page.</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Sean Tinney, Demand Generation Manager, AWeber</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The most highly engaged, highest converting customers come from SEO, in my experience.&#160; These are potential customers who are actively searching for a specific product or service.&#160;But in order for SEO to be effective, you need to do your research and add keywords to your landing page that provide the answer to what people are searching for.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Here at AWeber, we are providing marketing services to help our customers grow their business.&#160;So when I build a landing page using our <a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/landing-page-builder.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=landingpagebuilder\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">AWeber landing page builder</a>, I make sure I’m using keywords that potential customers might be searching for.&#160; </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The more targeted or specific your keywords, the greater the likelihood of success.&#160;Very popular terms and keywords tend to be highly competitive, so search terms that are more specific tend to be easier to rank for. </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Measure, track results, and adjust course.</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Cathy McPhillips, VP of Marketing at Content Marketing Institute&#160;</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>We promote our landing pages a number of ways: blog post calls-to-action (CTAs), banner ads on our website, social media, email promotions, and through our webinar speakers and Content Marketing Institute team members. Each of these tactics has a sourced URL so we’re able to evaluate the effectiveness and the timing promotions.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>For example, if we’re posting on social media four weeks before a webinar, but 90% of our webinar signups through social media happen 28 hours before the event, then we shouldn’t be posting on social media so early. We also are able to see our key influencers which helps us fine tune our distribution strategy.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>We also use different copy for each of our promotions to the landing page, because this page or webinar will appeal to our personas in different ways. We have found that pulling data, discussing key takeaways, or asking questions that the landing page will answer are the best ways to engage our customers and to get them to take that next step toward conversion.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Build your own landing page today.</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber’s Landing Page Builder makes creating a landing page for your business easy. <a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/free.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=landingpageblog-free\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Get started with AWeber Free</a> to start building your landing page and growing your list today.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph --><p>The post <a Lists\" srcset=\"http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/Blog-Cover-1200x675-1.png 1200w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/Blog-Cover-1200x675-1-300x169.png 300w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/Blog-Cover-1200x675-1-1024x576.png 1024w, http://6elrmjmsbs335jwbeybarrry.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/Blog-Cover-1200x675-1-768x432.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p><p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You want peace of mind when sending your messages to your subscribers.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That means making sure that your email is delivered to your subscribers’ inboxes. But it also means knowing you’re sending legally compliant marketing emails.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you’re just starting a business — or just starting to use email marketing to promote your business — it can be really tempting to buy an email list. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You want to grow your business — and </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">fast. </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What better way than to start promoting your business to a large audience?</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here’s the ugly truth: cutting corners and buying an email list will hurt you and your business in more ways than one. It’s why AWeber and other reputable email services will </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">not </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">allow you to import a purchased email list. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Read on to learn everything you need to know about buying an email list. And how to grow an email following the right way. </span></p>\n<h2><strong>Why AWeber does not allow you to import a purchased list.</strong></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Here at </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=blogcontent&#38;utm_content=blogcontent082218purchasedlists\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">AWeber</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, we have a group of trained specialists on our Best Practices team that monitors your </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/email-deliverability.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">email deliverability</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> 24/7. Our Best Practices team ensures AWeber provides you the </span><a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204027366-How-good-is-your-Email-Deliverability-\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">highest deliverability rates in the email marketing industry</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. We help you make it into the inbox, and not the spam folder.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That means our Best Practices team is on the lookout for AWeber customers importing or sending messages to purchased email lists. Purchased lists are directly against </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/service-agreement.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">AWeber’s Terms of Service</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and can result in a closure of your account.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And they come with big problems: Sending messages to a purchased email list can cause significant damage to your marketing initiatives, hurt your chances of making it into the inbox, and ruin all of your hard work.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Plus, penalties for sending unsolicited email to a purchased list could range anywhere from </span><a href=\"https://www.itbusiness.ca/news/casls-1-1-million-spam-fine-outlier-or-the-new-normal/54244\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">hefty fines</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> to even </span><a href=\"https://www.spamtitan.com/blog/penalties-for-spamming/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">jail time</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, depending on your country’s </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/meet-the-anti-spam-laws-from-around-the-world.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">anti-spam laws</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<h2><strong>Is it legal to buy email lists?</strong></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When it comes to email marketing, there are a few laws you need to know that will help you make informed decisions — especially about purchasing email lists. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">GDPR — or the General Data Protection Regulation — is a European law that directly states that email subscribers </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">must </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">opt-in to receive your emails with active consent. Even if you’re not based in Europe, if have customers or subscribers in Europe, you must comply with GDPR. And</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, it must be clear what your subscribers can expect to receive from you. </span></p>\n<p><b>Buying an email list is a clear violation of GDPR.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Want to learn more about GDPR and what it means for your business? Check out </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/your-gdpr-email-marketing-playbook-how-to-prepare-for-the-new-eu-data-law.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your GDPR + Email Marketing Playbook</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But there are also a few other laws that reinforce why you should never buy an email list. </span></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.ftc.gov/tips-advice/business-center/guidance/can-spam-act-compliance-guide-business\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The CAN-SPAM Act </span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">is a United States law that regulates commercial email. While it doesn’t actually prohibit someone from buying and selling email addresses, it does prohibit sending bulk unsolicited emails. And if you’re sending to a purchased email list, that’s exactly what you’re doing. You would be in violation of the law.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Plus, the </span><a href=\"https://oag.ca.gov/privacy/ccpa\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">California Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA)</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, which went into effect on January 1, 2020, protects the personal information of California residents. Businesses need to honor requests from California residents to “access, delete, and opt-out of sharing or selling their information.” </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">By purchasing an email list, you can't be sure that a vendor has followed those rules. And, California is only the first state to enact a law like this — others are likely not far behind.</span></p>\n<h2><b>Why you should never buy an email list</b></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our Best Practices team doesn’t only catch bad actors using purchased lists — even well-intentioned businesses can fall into the trap of buying email lists. After all, a purchased list sounds like a great idea in theory; you feel like you can start marketing your product or service right away to a list of subscribers, instead of having to grow your list from scratch, right?</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Wrong. Simply put, buying an email list will hurt you more than it will help you. </span></p>\n<p>Some companies make money by offering new email marketers a “shortcut” to building their email lists. So they compile email address lists and advertise them as:</p>\n<ul>\n<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"Targeted\"</span></li>\n<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"Opt-in\"</span></li>\n<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"Verified\"</span></li>\n<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"Clean\" (a clue that purchasing lists is inherently dirty)</span></li>\n<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">\"Real Time\"</span></li>\n</ul>\n<p>Here are some examples:</p>\n<p><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-87720\" src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/07/08212018-Article-Post-3.jpg\" alt=\"company selling purchased email list\" width=\"740\" height=\"630\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-83643\" src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2008/07/Screen-Shot-2017-05-23-at-4.46.42-PM.png\" alt=\"\" width=\"1237\" height=\"558\" /></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When buying a list of email addresses, you don’t have proof of who else may have also purchased those addresses, what list those subscribers signed up for originally, or the date those subscribers signed up. While the company selling the list may say it’s “Opt-In” or “Verified,” you have no idea what content they first signed up for.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you send messages to a purchased email list, you don’t have explicit opt-in to be emailing those subscribers. Explicit opt-in — meaning subscribers actively and knowingly gave you permission to email them (i.e. filling out a sign up form on your website) — is required for a quality list, says AWeber’s Best Practices Manager, Josh Smith. “If you don’t have explicit opt-in, you are bound to have problems,” he explains.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And fair warning: Confirmation does not equal permission.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The </span><a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204028656-What-is-confirmed-opt-in-\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">confirmation message</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is one of the first emails you send to subscribers when they are added to your mailing list. In it, a subscriber can click on a link to confirm that they requested information from you.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">However, you can’t just send a confirmation message to a purchased list — because they never gave you permission to email them in the first place. They never requested to be on your email list. Confirmation can only be used as a second step in order to build a more engaged list.</span></p>\n<h3><strong>So how do email addresses end up on purchased email lists? </strong></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Any email address can end up in a purchased email list database. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Vendors that sell email lists scrape email addresses off old lists, get attendee lists from conferences, and pick them off websites that have nothing to do with your specific business. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This means the people you’re emailing may not be interested in what you do at all. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For instance, your purchased list may claim to have opted-in for your gardening tips. In reality, however, those email addresses signed up for sports news and updates.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The result: The subscribers on your purchased list have no interest in your gardening content. They never open your messages, or, worse, they mark your messages as spam.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Even if the vendor collected the email addresses legitimately, none of the subscribers on the purchased list are aware of you or your business. They don’t expect to hear from you, and are more likely to mark you as spam.</span></p>\n<h2><strong>How buying email lists will hurt you and your business</strong></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Most subscribers know if they have requested specific information from you or not. Sending unsolicited information to subscribers who did not request it can be damaging to your business and your deliverability.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Internet Service Providers (ISPs) — like Gmail, Hotmail, or Yahoo! — track if a subscriber opens an email, clicks a link, or reports a message as spam in their inbox.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If the </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-deliverability/getting-into-the-inbox-why-email-engagement-is-more-important-than-ever-for-email-deliverability.htm?utm_source=awemail&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=blogcontent&#38;utm_content=buyinglistdeliver0605\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">engagement is good</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> — meaning, a subscriber constantly opens your messages, forwards them, or clicks the links inside — this tells the ISP to route future emails straight to the inbox.</span></p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Related: Not sure if your email open or click-through rates are good? </span></i><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/2020-report/?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=2020research&#38;utm_content=aweberblogpost\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Check out AWeber’s 2020 Email Marketing Statistics Repor</span></i></a><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">t to discover average email engagement.</span></i></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">However, if a subscriber is unengaged, then an ISP will route your emails to the spam folder. And if a large portion of your subscribers are unengaged — which will most likely be the case with a purchased list — it can </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-deliverability/2-major-reasons-why-you-should-care-about-email-deliverability.htm?utm_source=awemail&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=blogcontent&#38;utm_content=buyinglistsopt0606\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">hurt your sending reputation</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. All of your messages may end up in the spam folder whether a subscriber wants to read your emails or not.</span></p>\n<h2><strong>What to do instead of buying an email list</strong></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There are other great ways to </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">grow your list</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> that don’t involve buying email addresses.</span></p>\n<h3><strong>Build a strong brand</strong></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Successful businesses are built on strong brands that people love. And strong brands are built on exceptional products that solve a problem for your unique audience. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That’s the winning formula. Offer a valuable product or service, build and deliver it with care, and look for every opportunity to delight your customers.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Buying an email list skips too many crucial steps in building a strong brand. With a purchased list, unprepared recipients aren’t likely to think, “Oh gosh, I was just hoping for yet another offer from a company I don’t know! Let me click over to their site and buy something!”</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you were hoping to sell to this list, you might want to adjust your expectations.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Convincing someone to opt in to receiving emails from you means earning their trust, and the only way to do that is by solving their problems, providing value, and treating them with respect. That takes time and hustle.</span></p>\n<h3><strong>Create a sign up form for your website. </strong></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Collect email addresses from people who visit your website. Make sure your </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/sign-up-forms.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">sign up form</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is accessible and visible across the site to make it easy for people to find and subscribe. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You’ll see higher engagement and better results since your subscribers signed up for the content themselves.</span></p>\n<h3><strong>Create a landing page to drive subscribers to.</strong></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t have a website? No problem. A </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/landing-page-builder.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">landing page</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is a fantastic way to promote your business and encourage sign ups. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">While navigation is limited on a landing page, that’s a good thing for email sign ups. Write your landing page in a way that explains the value of signing up for your email list clearly and highlights your sign up form on the page. </span></p>\n<h3><strong>Offer a lead magnet to entice people to sign up for your list.</strong></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> A lead magnet is a freebie or incentive that encourages people to sign up for your email list. In exchange for their email address, you give them something valuable that solves a problem for them.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For instance, if you’re a vegan health coach, a guide like ‘My top 5 vegan recipes for weight loss,” could be a valuable offer to your audience. If they want the guide, they’ll gladly hand over their email address and will be eager to hear from you.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can get incredibly creative with your lead magnets. Offer calendars, guides, checklists, recipes, the list is endless as long it’s valuable and solves a problem for your audience. </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/22-brilliant-lead-magnets-that-are-growing-email-lists-right-now.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get 22 more brilliant lead magnet ideas. </span></a></p>\n<h3><strong>Turn your social media following into email subscribers. </strong></h3>\n<p><a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204027926-How-do-I-add-a-Sign-Up-Form-to-my-Facebook-page-\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Add your sign up form to your Facebook page</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> and publish the AWeber hosted URL to your sign up form or landing page as a pinned Tweet. Or, include a link to sign up for your newsletter or email list in your Instagram bio. </span></p>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><strong>Ask your personal relationships to sign up for your email list.</strong> </span></h3>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">There’s no better way to spread the word about your business and email newsletter than through your personal relationships. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Let friends and family know about your venture. Make it easy for them to forward your email and ask them to help spread the word. </span></p>\n<h2><strong>Want to learn more about how to get more subscribers and grow your business without buying an email list? </strong></h2>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Get all the tools and resources you need to become an email pro with our guide, “</span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/grow-your-business.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How to Grow Your Business with Email Marketing</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.”</span></p>\n<p> </p>\n\n<!-- wp:html -->\n<script type=\"application/ld+json\">\n{\n  \"@context\": \"https://schema.org\",\n  \"@type\": \"FAQPage\",\n  \"mainEntity\": [{\n    \"@type\": \"Question\",\n    \"name\": \"Is it legal to buy email lists?\",\n    \"acceptedAnswer\": {\n      \"@type\": \"Answer\",\n      \"text\": \"When it comes to email marketing, there are a few laws you need to know that will help you make informed decisions — especially about purchasing email lists. GDPR — or the General Data Protection Regulation — is a European law that directly states that email subscribers must opt-in to receive your emails with active consent. Even if you’re not based in Europe, if have customers or subscribers in Europe, you must comply with GDPR. The CAN-SPAM Act is a United States law that regulates commercial email. While it doesn’t actually prohibit someone from buying and selling email addresses, it does prohibit sending bulk unsolicited emails. Plus, the California Consumer Privacy Act (CCPA), which went into effect on January 1, 2020, protects the personal information of California residents. Businesses need to honor requests from California residents to “access, delete, and opt-out of sharing or selling their information.”\"\n    }\n  },{\n    \"@type\": \"Question\",\n    \"name\": \"Should I buy an email list?\",\n    \"acceptedAnswer\": {\n      \"@type\": \"Answer\",\n      \"text\": \"No. When you send messages to a purchased email list, you don’t have explicit opt-in to be emailing those subscribers. Explicit opt-in — meaning subscribers actively and knowingly gave you permission to email them (i.e. filling out a sign up form on your website) — is required for a quality list.\"\n    }\n  },{\n    \"@type\": \"Question\",\n    \"name\": \"How do email addresses end up on purchased email lists?\",\n    \"acceptedAnswer\": {\n      \"@type\": \"Answer\",\n      \"text\": \"Any email address can end up in a purchased email list database. Vendors that sell email lists scrape email addresses off old lists, get attendee lists from conferences, and pick them off websites that have nothing to do with your specific business. This means the people you’re emailing may not be interested in what you do at all.\"\n    }\n  },{\n    \"@type\": \"Question\",\n    \"name\": \"How do I build a list without buying an email list?\",\n    \"acceptedAnswer\": {\n      \"@type\": \"Answer\",\n      \"text\": \"Build a strong brand. Create a sign up form for your website. Create a landing page to drive subscribers to. Offer a lead magnet to entice people to sign up for your list. Turn your social media following into email subscribers. Ask personal relationships to sign up for your email list.\"\n    }\n  }]\n}\n</script>\n<!-- /wp:html -->\n\n<!-- wp:html -->\n<script type=\"application/ld+json\">\n{\n  \"@context\": \"https://schema.org\",\n  \"@type\": \"BlogPosting\",\n  \"mainEntityOfPage\": {\n    \"@type\": \"WebPage\",\n    \"@id\": \"https://blog.aweber.com/email-deliverability/buying-email-lists-the-ugly-truth.htm\"\n  },\n  \"headline\": \"The Ugly Truth About Buying Email Lists\",\n  \"description\": \"Cutting corners and buying an email list will hurt you and your business in more ways than one. Your subscribers are animal lovers — but some of them want to receive information about cats, while others want to receive information about dogs.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>With dynamic email content, you can send one email that delivers dog information to dog lovers and cat information to cat lovers.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/j7ITkTkOp58A7T17-NHqpoAsbNHBS936IKb_8r8qfc7Y2qHz_n0nbNn__t2kWbLwcC-YKCNDwLh7Yr9Dt46t9xIcsIThu_CJ_RINbNORLKmSDfU_WywcY7HRLxy77IGhNQChB8GA\" alt=\"custom_field.gif\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Personalizing your emails in this way can significantly increase engagement <em>and</em> save time. In fact, 81% of content marketers believe that interactive <a href=\"https://contentmarketinginstitute.com/2016/07/interactive-content-research/\">content grabs attention more effectively</a> than static content.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>It eliminates the need to write separate emails for different audiences. Instead, you create one email and put in content that varies by the audience segment.  </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>\"You can also use dynamic content in the subject line to catch attention within the inbox. Let's say you have a subscriber that visited a product page on your website, but the sunglasses, for example, were out of stock. If your ecommerce platform is integrated with AWeber, you can send an automated email to notify the right group of subscribers when you have more sunglasses in stock. -->\n<p><a href=\"http://www.laurieconrod.com/home-page-llc\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">Freedom Digital Marketing</a> founder Laurie Conrod helps real estate agents and other entrepreneurs grow their businesses.&#160; She teaches entrepreneurs how to automate their lead generation using direct response marketing and social media marketing.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>She knew there had to be a better way to grow her small business efficiently and her client base than the time-consuming task of traditional prospecting. \"I didn't want to prospect people anymore for lead generation. I wanted to learn how to tap into the millions of people that are on the Internet,\" said Conrod.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>She needed a way to entice potential clients to attend her free training and then capture these attendees to offer her digital marketing services. This strategy would enable Conrod to demonstrate her knowledge and skills to prospects in a low-risk format. However, she lacked a reliable platform to manage her growing client database and power her online training.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Until she came across <a href=\"https://www.aweber.com?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=customersuccess&#38;utm_content=freedomdigitalmarketing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">AWeber</a> and <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/new-features/new-sign-up-forms-and-gotowebinar-integration.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=customersuccess&#38;utm_content=freedomdigitalmarketing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">GoToWebinar</a>.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Here are the 6 steps Conrod followed to grow her audience without prospecting.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 1: Create an engaging lead magnet</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod uses webinars as her lead magnet to attract prospects. \"The goal as an entrepreneur is to build 'know, like, and trust' with people as quickly as possible in order to make sales. Letting them see me on a webinar, how I present myself and my expertise is one of the fastest ways for people to get to know, like, and trust me. GoToWebinar has been such a powerful platform for me to use,\" says Conrod.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>She usually offers free training on topics such as online lead generation, social media marketing, and email marketing. In Conrod's training, she teaches realtors the basics of running Facebook campaigns and social media marketing.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber provides a direct integration with GoToWebinar, which means you can instantly add GoToWebinar registrants directly to your AWeber list.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:core-embed/youtube {\"url\":\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sH_rhN8fX10?autoplay=1\",\"type\":\"video\",\"providerNameSlug\":\"youtube\",\"className\":\"wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-embed-youtube wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\"><div class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\">\nhttps://www.youtube.com/watch?v=sH_rhN8fX10\n</div><figcaption>Click the video box to start the video. Step by step instructions listed below.</figcaption></figure>\n<!-- /wp:core-embed/youtube -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Step by Step on how to integrate GoToWebinar with AWeber</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li>In your account, click the <a rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" href=\"https://www.aweber.com/users/apps?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=customersuccess&#38;utm_content=freedomdigitalmarketing\" target=\"_blank\">Integrations</a> link in the upper right corner of the page.</li><li>Find the GoToWebinar integration and click on it.&#160;</li><li>On the next page, you will want to click the \"Connect\" button.</li><li>You'll then be asked to log into your GoToWebinar account. After doing so, click the \"Allow\" button to grant access for the integration.</li><li>Now that the app is connected, it's time to create your GoToWebinar automations in AWeber. To do so, click the \"Create an Automation\" button.</li><li>Using the drop down menu provided, select the webinar you would like to connect with AWeber. Once selected, click the \"Next\" button.</li><li>Next, select the AWeber list you would like your webinar registrants to be added to. Then, click the \"Submit\" button.</li><li>At this point, your webinar is connected to the previously selected AWeber list. Registrants will automatically be added to your AWeber list.</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 2: Promote the lead magnet to drive sign ups</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod promotes her lead magnet through paid ads on Facebook and Instagram. The paid advertising drives prospects to a landing page to collect their contact information.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91571,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><a href=\"http://www.laurieconrod.com/home-page-llc\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Site-1-Video-Save-My-Spot-Button-1024x723.png\" alt=\"Freedom Digital Marketing landing page for a free webinar.\" class=\"wp-image-91571\"/></a></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod includes three additional essential elements on her landing page.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>#1. A sign up form to collect email addresses</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91572,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Site-4-Registration-Form-1024x681.png\" alt=\"Freedom Digital Marketing sign up form.\" class=\"wp-image-91572\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>#2.&#160; Information about what she will cover in the webinar</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91573,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Site-2-Webinar-Countdown-1024x490.png\" alt=\"Freedom Digital Marketing list on what will be covered in an upcoming webinar.\" class=\"wp-image-91573\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>#3. Social proof to demonstrate how past attendees found value</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91574,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Site-3-Facebook-Responses-1024x735.png\" alt=\"Freedom Digital Marketing social proof of the value of the webinar with attendees testimonials.\" class=\"wp-image-91574\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 3: Grow an email list</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>When these prospects register for the webinar, they are immediately added to an email list she has set up on AWeber's email marketing platform.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>\"AWeber helps me build an email list. It is really the most crucial part of building a business. And that's true for any business: brick and mortar, retail, restaurants, or carpet cleaning. If you're building an email list, you can always generate new revenue from your client base and potential clients. If you're not building your list, you're leaving money on the table,\" says Conrod.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><strong>Pro Tip:</strong> &#160;<a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/grow-your-email-list-with-webinars.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=customersuccess&#38;utm_content=freedomdigitalmarketing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">5&#160; tactics for promoting your Webinar and growing your email audience.</a></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 4: Segment the List</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod promotes webinars to her customers and prospects.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>To ensure the right messages are sent to the intended audience, Conrod segments the list to send appropriate email messages to her subscribers.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>\"My mission is to help people automate their lead generation so that their potential clients are coming to them. Entrepreneurs need to learn that 'the money is in their lists.' AWeber is instrumental because you build your email list and then automate your follow-up with as many potential clients as possible. I help entrepreneurs learn how to do that,\" said Conrod.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Need segmentation inspiration? There are<strong> </strong><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/16-ways-to-segment-subscribers.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=customersuccess&#38;utm_content=freedomdigitalmarketing\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">16 ways to segment subscribers in AWeber</a>.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 5: Automate email campaigns</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod emails her new clients almost daily with an automated email sequence. She has found that including links to watch videos is a really good practice because it allows people to know, like, and trust her much faster than just reading emails. </p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91600,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NEW-Email-1-Real-Estate-Leads-On-Auto-Pilotv2-617x1024.png\" alt=\"An example of Freedom Digital Marketing automated email sequence.\" class=\"wp-image-91600\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod likes to give a lot of value and avoid salesy language in her email and social media. \"You can't constantly be pitching people and expect them to continue to open your emails because they'll get sick of it. We have to let people see our expertise and the value that we give so that they want to do business with us,\" says Conrod.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>After the training, she continues to engage with her list by sharing the video recording through AWeber.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91601,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NEW-Email-2-Ding-Ding-FYIv2-690x1024.png\" alt=\"An example of an email sharing a link to watch a Freedom Digital Marketing video.\" class=\"wp-image-91601\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Step 6: Create a system for success</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Conrod found a winning formula: a combination of AWeber and GoToWebinar. GoToWebinar became the driver of her lead generation strategy. AWeber handled the backend of her process and allowed her to connect with her audience to create remarkable experiences.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>\"You don't have to be a PhD to have a skill that you can sell online, but you do need a reliable system to do it well. Having a system is essential to build a six-figure and beyond business,\" says Conrod.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Ready to grow your business?</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading
