1200px) 100vw, 1200px\" /></p><!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Did you know that <a href=\"https://searchengineland.com/7-conversion-rate-truths-will-change-landing-page-optimization-strategy-191083\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">less than 3%</a> of people who visit your website or landing page for the first time will buy from you?&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>But, when you build a connection with your audience and learn what interests them, you can send them emails with personalized content that cater to their needs and interests.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Imagine how your business could grow if you were able to communicate with your subscribers about what they found interesting on your website.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>What if you could even trigger an automated, personalized message if an item was left in their shopping cart but never purchased?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Well, now you can when you use AWeber’s Page Hit Automation feature to track webpage visitors.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The best part is you don’t even need a website to start using AWeber’s Page Hit Automation. <a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/landing-page-builder.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=pagehitautomation\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">The AWeber Landing Page Builder</a> automatically includes everything you need to get started.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>How Can Your Web Traffic be Monetized? </h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Webpage tracking with AWeber's Page Hit Automation lets you tag email subscribers who visit certain website pages or landing pages after clicking on a link in your email.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>For instance, let’s say you send your subscribers a link to your website. If a subscriber links the link to your website, but then navigates to a page to check out the products you’re selling, you can apply a web tag which could indicate that subscriber as “interested” since they expressed interest in your products by hitting that web page.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Pretty neat, right?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Here’s how it works: all you have to do is add a piece of javascript code on your website to gather data. The javascript is invisible to subscribers who visit your website page.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Don’t worry, adding javascript code to your website is not complicated at all.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber has <a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/360045940114?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=pagehitautomation\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">step-by-step instructions</a> and our Customer Solutions team is always there to help 24/7 by phone, chat, or email if you get stuck.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Plus, if you use AWeber Landing Pages, enabling Page Hit Automation is even easier.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>“All AWeber Landing Pages come automatically equipped with the requisite javascript to tag subscribers on page hit, so you <strong>don't even need a website</strong> to use it. That means, without even having a website, you can use Page Hit Automation to start campaigns, stop campaigns, and add/remove subscribers from your dynamic segments,” says Chris Fox, AWeber Junior Product Manager.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Once the javascript is in place, you can add web tags for event tracking or behavior tracking on your website or AWeber landing page.&#160;&#160;And then begin monetizing your web traffic.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91748,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Page-Hit-Automation-Image-1-Applying-Tag-812x1024.png\" alt=\"Screen shot of adding a web tag for AWeber's Page Hit Automation.\" class=\"wp-image-91748\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>When a visitor takes a specific action, a tag is generated and automatically added to that individual's contact information in your AWeber account.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>4 ways to use web tracking to increase sales </h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Here are 4 of the most common ways AWeber’s customers are using website visitor tracking with our Page Hit Automation to monetize their web traffic.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Track subscribers’ on-site action using tags</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Website visitor tracking helps you learn how many subscribers return to your website or AWeber landing page, and what they click, abandon in their cart, or purchase.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>How users interact with your website or landing page helps you define your marketing campaign's goals. Do you want to set up a campaign to grow your email list, generate leads for a webinar, boost sales for a particular product, or test a lead magnet?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Or, you may want to send a welcome message to a first time subscriber and visitor. If you know they have an interest in a particular service, product, or piece of content, a tailored message can go a long way to convince them to buy.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Create dynamic segments based on tags</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You can use webpage tags to <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/case-studies/creating-custom-segments.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=pagehitautomation\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">create dynamic subscriber segments</a>. When you set up a dynamic segment, it eliminates the need to manually set search criteria every time you send an email to a particular audience segment. Dynamic segments instantly add new subscribers with the same search criteria.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>For example, you may set up a segment to automatically add any subscriber (new or existing) that purchases a particular product or clicked on a specific link on your website or AWeber landing page.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>That segment is perfect for sending relevant and personalized content to help drive more sales and build a more intimate and impactful relationship with that subscriber.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/v4d5zk6l3j.jsonp\" async=\"\"></script><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p>\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_v4d5zk6l3j seo=false videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\">&#160;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Trigger automated email campaigns based on on-site actions</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>A great example of a customer successfully using this technique is <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/case-studies/how-this-photographer-grew-his-email-list.htm?utm_source=awblog&#38;utm_medium=email&#38;utm_campaign=product&#38;utm_content=pagehitautomation\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">James Maher Photography</a>.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Maher sends subscribers an automated campaign based on the content they downloaded from his site. Maher sends all visitors who downloaded a particular piece of content an in-depth automated email to share information and tips, build relationships with new subscribers, and promote paid products.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Maher only has to set up the automated campaign once and then AWeber handles the rest.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91749,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><a href=\"https://www.jamesmaherphotography.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Page-Hit-Automation-Image-2-James-Maher-Email.png\" alt=\"Example of an email sent by James Maher Photography\" class=\"wp-image-91749\"/></a></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Trigger Cart Abandonment campaigns using Web Tracking</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Have you ever visited a website, put an item in your cart but decided to hold off purchasing, and later that day received an email from the company, reminding you of the item you purchased (and it may even include a code for a discount to purchase)? &#160; That company monetizes their web traffic using technology similar to AWeber's Page Hit Automation to track your behavior and send you relevant information.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>There’s tangible value to setting up an automated campaign for cart abandonment, too. Nearly half of all cart abandonment emails are opened, and over a <a href=\"https://www.elasticpath.com/blog/cart-abandonment-stats-infographic\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">third of those clicks lead to a purchase back on site</a>.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber even has a prebuilt abandoned cart message that you can easily automate when a cart abandonment tag is added to your subscribers' contact information.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/ewk6srif5d.jsonp\" async=\"\"></script><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p>\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_ewk6srif5d seo=false videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\">&#160;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p></p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>“My favorite use of Page Hit Automation is when people connect it to an Abandoned Cart flow. If a user never reaches the receipt page and they left an item in a cart, an Abandoned cart tag triggers a campaign message to be sent in a few hours later, urging them to return and complete the purchase,” says Fox.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>4 Reasons why you should use AWeber's Web Tracking Tool&#160;</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li>You want to <strong>wow</strong> your subscribers by sending them the perfect message at the ideal time!</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>One size fits all, generic emails are not going to cut it in today's personalized world. Your subscribers and customers want to feel appreciated and valued. With the data from Page Hit Automation, AWeber's marketing automation allows you to deliver the perfect message to the right people.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true,\"start\":2} -->\n<ol start=\"2\"><li>Understand your customer’s journey to move a passive prospect to an engaged customer.</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>“Page Hit Automation provides a deep level of insight into how users are interacting with your content <em>beyond</em> email. It ties together how your email performance is connected with your website or AWeber landing page performance. It helps you understand how effective your entire sales funnel is and where you may have room for improvement,\" says Fox.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true,\"start\":3} -->\n<ol start=\"3\"><li>Understand what content interests a subscriber so you can send more relevant emails to move them closer to a purchase.</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You will start to see strong preferences and trends to identify if you need to provide more content on your website to answer questions and how you may want to bucket subscribers to send more personalized and relevant content.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true,\"start\":4} -->\n<ol start=\"4\"><li>Identify your best prospects&#160;</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Page Hit automation makes it easy to track website visitors who made it to your product pages or shopping cart but never hit the receipt page. With Campaigns, you can send them an automated cart abandonment email or win-back email to drive your audience back to the cart. Track how the campaign message performs, and if they don't bite, maybe you need to sweeten the deal with a discount coupon. AWeber drag-and-drop email builder includes an easy to use coupon element and prebuilt templates that already include the coupon element.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":91750,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Say-Thank-You-Template-Image-1-1024x790.png\" alt=\"Example of a prebuilt AWeber email template with the coupon element.\" class=\"wp-image-91750\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>How to set up Website Visitor Tracking</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you are using one of AWeber’s landing pages, you can skip to the video below, since the javascript tracking code is already part of the landing page.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you have a website, you need to set up your website domain in AWeber's Email Web Analytics.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>By adding a short snippet of code to your website, you can also track the pages you want. AWeber includes easy to follow, <a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204029756-How-do-I-install-Email-Web-Analytics-\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">step-by-step instructions</a> on how to install Email Web Analytics. Once you add AWeber's Email Web Analytics to your webpage, follow the video below to set up your Page Hit Automations.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Set up your Page Hit Automations&#160;</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<p><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/embed/medias/dlmjw12szh.jsonp\" async=\"\"></script><script src=\"https://fast.wistia.com/assets/external/E-v1.js\" async=\"\"></script></p>\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_padding\" style=\"padding:56.25% 0 0 0;position:relative;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_responsive_wrapper\" style=\"height:100%;left:0;position:absolute;top:0;width:100%;\">\n<div class=\"wistia_embed wistia_async_dlmjw12szh seo=false videoFoam=true\" style=\"height:100%;position:relative;width:100%\">&#160;</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li>Go to the List Options tab on your AWeber dashboard and click \"List Automation.\"</li><li>Return to the AWeber List Automation page and click \"Add Automation\" to apply tags to a Page Hit.</li><li>You can either put in a URL that is an exact match or use ‘contains’ to track multiple pages on a given website</li><li>Next, select the action and result. You can only choose \"Page Hit\" and \"Add/Remove Tag.\"</li><li>Input any tags that you would like to add to your subscribers when they visit this page.</li><li>Input any tags that you would like to remove from your subscribers. Once complete, click \"Save.\"</li><li>Click save</li><li>After you save, you will see your automation rule under the \"Page Hit Automations\" section.</li><li>Select the campaign you want to automate.</li><li>Click “Replace trigger”, and select tag applied.</li><li>Enter the Page Hit Automation tag that will now trigger this campaign in the “Tag Applied” box on the left.&#160;</li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Now your automated campaigns are set up to trigger when a page hit automation tag is added to any of your subscriber’s contact information.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Start Monetizing Your Visitors today with AWeber’s Page Hit Automation!</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Does Page Hit Automation sound too good to be true? With its widespread reach and viral potential, it allows your business to connect with prospects in ways that no other marketing medium can.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But first you need a list of subscribers to send emails to. Whether you lack the time or the know-how to create quality emails, there are plenty of challenges that can prevent you from developing a healthy email list.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Fortunately, there are lots of easy ways to collect email addresses so that you reap the benefits of email marketing. We’ve gathered the best email list building tactics to grow subscribers in this guide. They are grouped below to help you:</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list --> \n<ul>\n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm#relationships\">Gain more subscribers through existing relationships</a></span></li>\n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm#website\">Learn how to get more emails from your website</a></span></li>\n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm#social\">Earn email subscribers from social and other sites</a></span></li>\n <li><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm#never-buy-list\">NEVER buy a list</a></li>\n <li><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/how-to-get-email-addresses.htm#monitor-and-track-email-performance\">Monitor and track email performance</a><br /></span></li>\n</ul> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\" id=\"relationships\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Collect more emails addresses through existing relationships</span></h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92364,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/06/Relationships.png\" alt=\"Collect more email addresses through existing relationships\" class=\"wp-image-92364\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">One of the easiest places to get started is by connecting with existing friends, colleagues, and any subscribers you have already. Not only is this a good place to start if you’re starting from scratch, but this can also feel the least scary. All you have to do is ask!</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Before you reach out to people, there are a few best practices you should keep in mind:</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list --> \n<ul>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Message people you have a relationship with.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> That random Facebook person you don’t remember meeting probably isn’t the best fit.</span></li>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Use WIIFM (What’s in it for me?”). </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Every time you message someone, make sure to tell them how your content, — whether it's a newsletter, email course, case study, or something else entirely — will benefit them or their friend.</span></li>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><b>Be yourself.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Tell your story, share your feelings, be vulnerable and real. People will subscribe and share your sign up form because they want to help YOU.</span></li>\n</ul> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1. Ask friends, family, and colleagues&nbsp;</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">One of the easiest marketing strategies to execute is to ask your current connections to join your list. Leveraging your network is a great way to steadily increase your email list, and often the best place to gain traction, especially in the beginning.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Although some of your connections may not be interested in the material themselves, they might know someone who is. Tell them you’re starting an email list. Explain the benefits and ask them if they know someone who would be interested in your focus areas(s).</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":4,\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h4 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Clearly articulate your purpose and the benefits.&nbsp;</span></h4> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When it comes time to send an </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/the-3-best-copywriting-formulas-for-email-marketing.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">email, avoid communicating like a robot</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Talk like you do in real life — it will help your customers relate to you better.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/new-features/8-new-email-templates-to-help-you-grow-your-business.htm\">Email templates</a> are a great starting point, but be sure to tailor it based on your relationship to the person and how you are asking. Depending on where a conversation is happening, people communicate very differently. When you text someone, you should be more casual than in an email. If you’re talking to someone in person, you shouldn’t be reading from a script you wrote beforehand.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">2. Ask customers and prospects&nbsp;</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When existing and prospective customers buy something from you or connect with you, verbally ask if they’d like to sign up for your email or newsletter. To entice them, you can provide something that could directly benefit them like a free ebook or kickoff template.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Grow your email list by asking customers you’re already speaking with on the phone. Tell them about what they can expect from your emails. It only takes a few seconds to jot down an email address. If you make “the big ask” five times a day for one work week, that’s 25 email addresses you didn’t have before you started, and 100 email addresses in just one month!</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">3. Capture emails from your email signature/closing</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How many people do you contact personally via email every day? These contacts might not be on your business email list yet, but that doesn’t mean you can’t suggest that they sign up to receive your email newsletter.Include a brief call-to-action and link to a form or </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/landing-page-builder.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">landing page</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> in your email signature.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This might not lead to a mountain of new email signups, but it is an easy, passive way to bring awareness if you’re emailing people regularly. Don’t forget to update other email signatures (e.g. a customer service email) and have team members update their signatures.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">4. Encourage forwarding</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Reach out to current subscribers and encourage them to share your email with people they know. Word-of-mouth is one of the oldest and most powerful means of advertising, and email offers the perfect venue for suggesting it to your subscribers. If they’re on your list and getting value from your messages, chances are they know others who would also benefit.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s important to make your emails easy to share and subscribe to. Update your template to include social sharing buttons. Devote a section of your newsletter to encourage subscribers to forward your message. Then, include a link to your sign-up page or hosted web form so that new readers can sign up directly from your email.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">5. Send postcards via snail mail</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Michelle Kemp, a fan of </span><a href=\"http://www.facebook.com/aweber\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">AWeber on Facebook</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, swears by sending postcards to prospects by mail:</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:quote {\"align\":\"center\"} --> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote has-text-align-center\">\n <p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">“Get your offline clients’ email addresses by mailing them a postcard with a free offer. Give them a website to go to and when they opt-in, give them your free content/giveaway that you promised. This works like a charm!”</span></p>\n</blockquote> \n<!-- /wp:quote --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you have their postal address, sending a client a personalized, handwritten note or postcard with a return address shows that you market transparently. It also puts a human touch on the otherwise technical task of collecting email addresses online.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\" id=\"website\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How to get more emails from your website</span></h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92365,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/06/Website.png\" alt=\"How to get more emails from your website\" class=\"wp-image-92365\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Oftentimes there are website improvement opportunities right under your nose. In many cases, an </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/plan-an-email-marketing-strategy.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">email marketing strategy</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> starts with a general, “subscribe to our newsletter” goal, then additional email capture goals are added piecemeal.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1. Offer freebies</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can also collect email addresses by offering freebies. </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nothing is more attractive to a potential customer than a free product (also called a </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/22-brilliant-lead-magnets-that-are-growing-email-lists-right-now.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">lead magnet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">) or a glance at a service that they don’t have yet.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">No matter what your newsletter is about, you are an expert in your field. Write up a quick guide to your industry, offer free templates or send an exclusive download of your latest podcast that’s only available to your email list.</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><br /></span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As long as your free gift is relevant to the content of your newsletter, it’s the perfect incentive for prospects who might be on the fence about signing up.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>2.</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> Make sure a form is present throughout your website</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><b><br /></b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">It’s best to have a </span><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/sign-up-forms.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">sign up form</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> on just about every page so that anyone who lands on your site is able to sign up quickly and painlessly for your emails. This is the simplest part of growing an email list, yet a common oversight for businesses focusing only on the homepage or a shortlist of “top pages.”</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The first (and sometimes only) interaction you have with people may happen on your website or blog. If you don’t make the most of that opportunity, it may be the last. When coming from Google, Facebook or a link shared on a blog, visitors will very rarely end up directly on your landing page. They’re probably directed to an article, or a specific page on your site that relates more closely to what they are looking for instead.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"align\":\"center\"} --> \n<p class=\"has-text-align-center\"><b><i>Related: </i></b><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/16-proven-sign-up-form-ideas-to-grow-your-email-list.htm\"><b><i>16 Proven Sign Up Form Ideas to Grow Your Email List</i></b></a></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>3. </b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Optimize your current form placement</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><b><br /></b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Even if you do have a sign up form accessible on every page on your site, test its location on various page templates. For example: if your blog posts only include a sign up form at the bottom of the post, the form isn’t getting nearly as much visibility as it would in the sidebar or halfway through posts.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Put your inline web form in an easy-to-find, consistent spot on every page of your site. In most cases, the web form should be above the fold (the section of your site that is visible without scrolling).</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>4</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Review what info you’re asking for and form messaging</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The email sign up process should be easy for the new subscriber and share what they can expect by signing up for your email list.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For starters, take a look at your current web form. Remember that getting all of their details up front will be helpful to you, but it isn’t an easy task for them.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Studies show that <a href=\"https://www.ventureharbour.com/how-form-length-impacts-conversion-rates/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\">form length will impact the number of signups</a> you receive. You should request only what you really need from them at this stage to prevent any barriers to entry.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">That doesn’t mean you can’t collect information to help you personalize your email send. But make sure that asking for that information isn’t causing a roadblock.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Also make sure you clearly communicate what your website visitors will receive after signing up, how often they will receive emails from you, and then stick to your commitment. Give visitors a reason to subscribe.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>5</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Experiment with Pop Ups</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Pop up forms can be a simple yet effective way to bring more attention to your email list. But it’s important to establish a few ground rules before getting started.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You don’t want to interrupt or annoy your website visitors with too many pop ups. Not all forms have to pop up in the middle of a screen and darken the background content. You can use a “sticky” form that unobtrusively remains on the bottom of the page as a user scrolls, or a slide-in form on the side of the screen.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can set the timing of your pop up forms to display after a user has been on the page for a certain time. Or set it so the form displays only when a user takes a specific action (e.g. their mouse showing exit-intent towards the X button) or when they reach the bottom of the page.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">6. Add incentives after a purchase</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Add an automatic incentive or CTA after a purchase is made (e.g. on your thank you page). Not every customer that purchases an item or service from you will always return.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can, however, work towards building customer loyalty with your emails. By leveraging the point of purchase to collect email addresses, you can bring them closer to becoming repeat customers.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">7. Run a contest to collect subscribers</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Contests are a perfect marketing strategy for drumming up excitement and attracting new subscribers. There are a number of tools available that can help you easily host a contest, such as </span><a href=\"https://gleam.io/examples\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Gleam.io</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> or </span><a href=\"https://www.viralsweep.com/examples/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">ViralSweep</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure you have a valuable prize, a relatively short entry period, and then don’t forget to promote it on your website and on social media. Setting a time period (e.g. a weeklong contest) instills a sense of urgency. This way they won’t assume they have plenty of time to sign up. And whatever your prize is, make sure it’s a valuable something-they-can’t-live-without item or offer.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\" id=\"social\">Earn emails from social and other sites</h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92366,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/06/Social.png\" alt=\"Earn emails from social and other sites\" class=\"wp-image-92366\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Now that you've asked existing relationships and optimized your website to capture more emails, you're ready to explore growth opportunities that extend beyond your site. Leveraging your social media following and reaching out to other sites in your industry should be some of the primary pillars of your growth strategy.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">1. Reach out to your social followers</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As a business owner, you probably already know a consistent social media presence can help you engage with customers, promote special offers, and build brand awareness. But did you know that you can use channels like Facebook and Twitter to grow your email marketing list, too?</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">By encouraging your social followers to sign up for your email list, you’re able to tap into an audience of people who are already interested in your business and what you have to say.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">While you can certainly post about the benefits of your email content (along with a link to your sign up form), you can also prove it by linking to your email archive.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>2</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Add a form to your Facebook business page</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Did you know that you can capture email addresses directly from Facebook? Simply integrate your email software with Facebook so that anyone visiting your page on the social networking site can easily subscribe to receive email updates. Here’s the </span><a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204027926-How-do-I-add-a-Sign-Up-Form-to-my-Facebook-page-\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">step-by-step integration instructions</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> for AWeber users.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>3</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Pin a tweet that could entice a sign up</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">While simply </span><a href=\"https://www.dummies.com/business/marketing/social-media-marketing/how-to-pin-a-tweet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">pinning a tweet</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> to the top of your profile feed that says “sign up for our newsletter” will likely have little impact, there are ways to show off reasons and opportunities to subscribe. Here are a few examples of what you can pin</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:list --> \n<ul>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Your most recent newsletter to provide a glimpse into what they could expect</span></li>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Impactful quotes, unique data, and other information from whitepapers/ebooks</span></li>\n <li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Upcoming webinars and events</span></li>\n</ul> \n<!-- /wp:list --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Create an even more desirable tweet with an image or GIF and easy-to-read copy.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph {\"align\":\"center\"} --> \n<p class=\"has-text-align-center\"><b><i>Related: </i></b><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/9-ways-to-grow-your-list-with-twitter.htm\"><b><i>9 Ways to Grow Your Email List with Twitter</i></b></a></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>4</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Invest in social advertising</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Social media is a powerful tool, especially when you can invest in it. LinkedIn and Facebook ad formats that specifically cater to email signups can help you reach your target audience.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t be afraid to play around with your ads and </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/the-ultimate-guide-to-email-a-b-testing.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">A/B test</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> different images, videos, GIFs and copy. Like email marketing campaigns, the only way to understand what resonates with your audience is to test, test, test!</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>5</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Don’t forget about YouTube (if you’re using it currently)</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Whether you’re active on YouTube and treat it like a social network or simply use it as a repository for video content, there is potential to earn email addresses.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Consider the best way to ask for an email—in terms of placement, the messaging of the ask, and the value they will receive. Most importantly, think about how to make it easy for users to subscribe.&nbsp;</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">YouTube offers a number of ways to include calls to action within the video area itself. You can also update the video’s “About” section to include a CTA. Always preview the live video first so you can place the most important information before the “Show More” truncation occurs.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>6</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Write for other industry blogs</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Guest writing is a great way to reach an audience you otherwise might not have. By contributing to other sites, you not only provide value to a new audience, but you also have the opportunity to find subscribers who might become some of your best customers.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} --> \n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\"><b>7</b><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. Cross-promote your list to another list</span></h3> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Have more than one list? Cross-promote your offer on one list to the other list.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The idea here is to convince people that there’s value to be obtained from your email list, and now’s the time to subscribe so they can get something immediately in return.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\" id=\"never-buy-list\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">But whatever you do, never buy a list</span></h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92367,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/06/Never-buy-a-list.png\" alt=\"Never buy a list\" class=\"wp-image-92367\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We get this question a lot when talking to new email marketers: “</span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How do I buy a list of emails?”</span></i></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The answer: </span><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-deliverability/buying-email-lists-the-ugly-truth.htm\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">don’t do it</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. The thought of building an email subscriber base can seem daunting, but the worst thing you can do is buy a list. (It’s actually illegal to sell email lists!)</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And when you purchase an email list, it hurts your email deliverability, because these emails did not subscribe to you and are likely to mark your messages as spam.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\" id=\"monitor-and-track-email-performance\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Monitor and track email performance</span></h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92368,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} --> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\">\n  <img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2010/06/monitor-and-track.png\" alt=\"Monitor and Track Email Performance\" class=\"wp-image-92368\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<!-- /wp:image --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Make sure you have the correct tracking in place on both your email newsletters and your website. The data you collect will allow you to identify top-performing content and inform decisions that help improve your strategy, which will result in more email addresses on your subscriber list. It’ll also help you find out which lead generation methods are producing the most impactful results.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Without the ability to track key metrics like conversion rate, it will be difficult to understand how your readers are interacting with your content and what they likely want to see more of in the future.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">To keep things simple (and free!) a tracking tool like Google Analytics can show your numbers and help you gauge performance. You can set this up in just a few minutes and start gathering in-depth analytics around your email and website traffic.</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} --> \n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">What are your list building tactics?</span></h2> \n<!-- /wp:heading --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Does one particular method help you attract new subscribers? Is there something that doesn’t work very well for your industry?</span></p> \n<!-- /wp:paragraph --> \n<!-- wp:paragraph --> \n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Once you have your list, now it’s time to start using email marketing to quickly grow your business. -->\n<p>People do business with brands they trust. But how can you build lasting trust among your audience? It starts with marketing.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The reason is simple: If your audience doesn't know about you, how can you begin establishing that trust in the first place?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>If you’re marketing your business, kudos. You may already have an edge on your competition. In fact, 58% of small business owners spend less than 5 hours a week on marketing. And <a href=\"https://www.searchenginejournal.com/50-of-small-businesses-do-not-have-a-marketing-plan/308777/#close\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\">50% of SMB owners do not have a marketing plan</a>.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You may be familiar with the <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/understanding-the-marketing-funnel-5-strategies-to-improve-your-email-marketing.htm\">marketing funnel</a>, in which marketing drives awareness, consideration, conversion (an order), loyalty (repeat buyers), and advocacy. So why would you not dedicate more time to marketing?</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Even if you don’t have a large marketing budget, experience with marketing, or a lot of&#160; time to devote to marketing, you don’t have to worry.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>This list of 10 free marketing ideas will help you worry less about the time, money, and know-how it takes to effectively market your business.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">Create Online Business Directories</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>An <a href=\"https://www.brightlocal.com/resources/the-ultimate-free-business-directory-list/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\">online business directory</a> is the digital version of the Yellow Pages phone book. It’s where people can find information on your business. Some business directories also allow people to leave reviews.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>There are several online business directories such as <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://www.google.com/business/\" target=\"_blank\">Google</a>, <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://yelp.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Yelp</a>, <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"http://manta.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Manta</a>, and <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://appleid.apple.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Apple Maps</a>.&#160; Setting up your online business directory is a great way for people to find your business and learn about your products and/or services.&#160; There are over 100 of these directories, however, some are industry-specific such as <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://www.zillow.com/\" target=\"_blank\">Zillow</a> (Real Estate), <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://www.tripadvisor.com/\" target=\"_blank\">TripAdvisor </a>(Travel), and <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://www.autotrader.com/\" target=\"_blank\">AutoTrader </a>(Automotive).</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92212,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Online-business-directories.png\" alt=\"Visual of online business directories\" class=\"wp-image-92212\"/></figure></div>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Find the ones that are general and specific to your industry and either create a business listing or claim your business. Yes, you may have a presence on these directories without even knowing it.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">Free Email Marketing Services</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Email marketing is ranked as the <a href=\"https://medium.com/@ThinkBigfish/email-is-the-most-effective-digital-marketing-channel-d644bc8bccf8#:~:text=Email%20lists%20work%20better%20and,reach%2C%20personalization%20and%20content%20value.\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\">top most effective marketing channel</a>, beating out social media and search engine marketing — making it one of the best ways to build strong relationships with your customers.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>There are email marketing platforms that offer free services, additional free tools, and are structured to help you do your email marketing more efficiently.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><a href=\"https://www.aweber.com/\">AWeber</a>, for example, is a powerfully-simple email marketing platform specifically designed for small businesses. If so, you may want to consider being active on LinkedIn. If you’re targeting consumers, you will have more work deciding which platform(s) to consider.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Once you’ve determined your target social media platform, be active, and encourage customers to like or follow you.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Then comes the fun part: post to your social media page. But make it interesting and interactive when possible. The more people who interact with your post through likes, comments, or shares, the more people will see your post both in your network of followers and outside.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Keep in mind people are following you because they had a good experience with your brand and want to learn more about you. Social media isn’t a place to force a hard sell. It’s a place to share.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Tips on what to post:</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:list -->\n<ul><li>Creative pictures of your products</li><li>A new product or service</li><li>Any interesting news about your business</li><li>Special offerings or coupons</li></ul>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You can even use specific social media platforms, like Facebook, to increase your email subscriber list. You can create a <a href=\"https://help.aweber.com/hc/en-us/articles/204027926-How-do-I-add-a-Sign-Up-Form-to-my-Facebook-page-\">sign up form for your page</a>, which will allow your Facebook follows to subscribe to your email list. Then you can email them newsletters, advice, and offers.&#160;&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Need help setting up this email marketing feature? If you’re an AWeber customer, our award-winner customer service team can help you.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">Use the Press to Help Spread the Word</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>A press release is a great way to boost your business. A well-written press release can give your company media exposure through news outlets (TV, print, and radio), influential bloggers, industry-specific publications, and more.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>A press release can bring you instant exposure, grow your sales potential, increase your brand awareness, improve your search engine results, and expand your target audience.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p><a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://www.cbsnews.com/news/how-to-write-a-press-release-with-examples/\" target=\"_blank\">Writing a press release</a> isn’t difficult. Once you find a structure that works for you, use that same format with every PR.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The most time-consuming part of issuing a press release is finding journalists who might be interested. To build this list, you’ll need to research and find a journalist who has previously written about your industry or topic.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"customTextColor\":\"#00539b\"} -->\n<h2 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#00539b\">Build Landing Pages to Collect New Leads</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The main Search Engine Optimization Strategy</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>The great thing about an effective search engine optimization (SEO) strategy is that you can be a small business and still own the top spot of a keyword search result.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Even if you’re a <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://ahrefs.com/blog/seo-basics/\" target=\"_blank\">beginner to SEO</a>, you can still structure your web pages to include targeted keywords you want to rank for.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3,\"customTextColor\":\"#af62ff\"} -->\n<h3 class=\"has-text-color\" style=\"color:#af62ff\">5 Simple Steps to Improve Your SEO</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:list {\"ordered\":true} -->\n<ol><li>Keyword research -&#160;<ul><li>Determine what keywords will be the focus of our webpage or blog post. There are a few <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://searchengineland.com/8-free-keyword-research-tools-for-seo-that-beat-their-paid-alternatives-318091\" target=\"_blank\">free keyword research tools</a> you can use to help.</li><li>Target <a rel=\"noreferrer nofollow noopener\" href=\"https://backlinko.com/hub/seo/long-tail-keywords\" target=\"_blank\">long-tail keywords</a> as these keywords tend to be less competitive as such you stand a better chance to rank for it.</li><li>Identify the type of phrases your customers might put into a search bar to find the answer on the internet.</li><li>See what other keyword suggestions make sense to add to your webpage or blog.</li></ul></li><li>Optimize Your Content for SEO<ul><li>Write your content to focus on these keywords.&#160;</li><li>In your first paragraph, you should mention the&#160; main keyword you want to target.</li></ul></li><li>Structure your page URL<ul><li>Your page URL extensions should have your focus keyword.&#160; For example, if your main or focus keyword is “How to paint a house”, your URL extension could be /how-to-paint-a-house/</li></ul></li><li>Add your title tag<ul><li>A title tag is your display title that appears in a search engine results page.</li><li>The title page structure should contain the title of your page, followed by a separator, like a dash or a line, and finally, your company name. Putting your company name in your title tag is important for brand recognition.</li><li>The title tag is what the reader would click from the search engine to read your content.</li><li>The optimal length is 50 - 60 characters.</li></ul></li><li>Add your meta description<ul><li>A meta description is the brief descriptive information shown below the title tag in a search engine results page.</li><li>The meta description needs to be an accurate description regarding the context of your page</li><li>The optimal length is no more than 160 characters.</li></ul></li></ol>\n<!-- /wp:list -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"align\":\"center\",\"id\":92218,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Title-tag-and-meta-description.png\" alt=\"Example of a title tag and meta description with an AWeber search\" class=\"wp-image-92218\"/></figure></div>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>These simple steps are just the beginning. <a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/22-brilliant-lead-magnets-that-are-growing-email-lists-right-now.htm\">Check out these 22 brilliant lead magnet ideas</a> that make growing your audience easy.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>Horizontal forms option</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Up until now, forms could only be displayed vertically. Now, display forms horizontally or vertically on your landing pages. This gives you the flexibility you need to display your sign up forms in the landing page builder in the style that best fits your landing page design.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>In the \"Form\" options, simply select the vertical or horizontal icon to choose your layout preference.&#160; The call to action button automatically formats to align with the form layout you selected.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/d3pg8WOi0IdFEfQmKsx6Myjja1XVEHoup8AxAdJoKZxRhJtm7_mmeGcbnZv-1Xy1vOwtoQ8GvukhVUW-LItiAgkNS27R2RrCmr0s2dMjca35xce32GAaBdDTU2yeciPZ-EBYyqe6\" alt=\"\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2>More design options! Margin, borders, drop shadows, and color background options</h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Create borders, rounded corners, drop shadows, and set margins for columns to create a more polished and customized landing page presentation. These new features allow you to take your landing page to the next level by easily adding card layouts or coupons for a special offer or discount.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\"><img src=\"https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/PshMv3qOwCLNCRNuIVnEUwLr1kkpQyZBEKrFIY6AkGTslP6bf_rggzV43Fsj4ZLVAJ5_-gfLCjBK1zg7quqK21QYYQDESz6B6oanKog7mFgqZ1UPsAIWC8rYhRX68YD9f0h6w9Ql\" alt=\"\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Borders</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>We added the ability to add borders for columns to personalize the look of your landing page further. In the \"Design\" sidebar on the right you can easily create a dotted, dashed, or solid border as well as adjust the width and color.&#160;</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92713,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GIF-2-Borders-Width-And-Color-GIF.gif\" alt=\"GIF on adding boarders\" class=\"wp-image-92713\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Corners and Drop Shadows</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>You can also adjust the appearance of your columns to have rounded corners. Select the \"Appearance\" option in the sidebar. Click either all corners or the specific corners. Then, adjust the corner or corner's appearance with the up and down arrows in the box.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber lets you add depth and variety to your existing landing pages with the new drop shadows features. You can now add drop shadows to their columns. Navigate to the row you want to update and go to the “Appearance” section. Then select the type of drop shadow you wish to apply.&#160; You can choose none, soft, or hard.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92714,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GIF-3-Corners-and-Drop-Shadow-Source-GIF.gif\" alt=\"GIF on Corners\" class=\"wp-image-92714\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading {\"level\":3} -->\n<h3>Background Colors</h3>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>To add variety to your landing pages consider changing the background color for individuals rows in your landing page.&#160; Simply navigate to that row and select the background color options, labeled \"BG Color\".&#160; Then choose the color you wish applied to that section.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:image {\"id\":92717,\"sizeSlug\":\"large\"} -->\n<figure class=\"wp-block-image size-large\"><img src=\"https://blog.aweber.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/GIF-4-Row-Background-Color-GIF.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-92717\"/></figure>\n<!-- /wp:image -->\n\n<!-- wp:heading -->\n<h2><a href=\"https://blog.aweber.com/email-marketing/what-to-look-for-with-free-email-marketing-service.htm\">Best free email and landing page marketing software&#160;</a></h2>\n<!-- /wp:heading -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>Our mission is simple: to deliver powerfully-simple email marketing tools to help small business owners and entrepreneurs — like you — grow your business.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:paragraph -->\n<p>AWeber Free is our completely free email marketing and landing pages plan — perfect for those who are just getting started or kicking off a passion project. We’ll give you everything you need to start building your audience today.</p>\n<!-- /wp:paragraph -->\n\n<!-- wp:buttons -->\n<div class=\"wp-block-buttons\"><!-- wp:button
